/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_CRExecutionPlan]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_CRExecutionPlan](
	@Flag [char](1),
	@ITCRExecID [int]=NULL,
	@ITCRID [int],
	@SysLandscape [int],
	@ExecutionStepName [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@ExecutionStepDesc [nvarchar](MAX) NULL,
	@AssignedTo [int] NULL,
	@StartDt [datetime] NULL,
	@EndDT [datetime] NULL,
	@Attachments [nvarchar](MAX) NULL,
	@Status [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	@ForwardStatus[nvarchar](50) NULL,
	@ForwardedTo [int] NULL,
	@ForwardedDt [datetime] NULL,
	@ReasonForwarded [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Remarks [nvarchar](2000) NULL,
	@PickedStatus [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	@PickedDt [datetime] NULL,
	@ActualStartDt [datetime] NULL,
	@ActualEndDt [datetime] NULL,
	@DependSysLandscape [int] NULL,
	@DependTaskID [int] NULL,
	@CreatedBy [int] NULL
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	If (@ForwardedTo<>'') 
	select @AssignedTo=@ForwardedTo

	IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert CR Approver Fields
	BEGIN 
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			INSERT INTO [IT].[CRExecutionPlan] (
			[ITCRID],
			[SysLandscape],
			[ExecutionStepName],
			[ExecutionStepDesc],
			[AssignedTo],
			[StartDt],
			[EndDT],
			[Attachments],
			[Status],
			[ForwardStatus],
			[ForwardedTo],
			[ForwardedDt],
			[ReasonForwarded],
			[Remarks],
			[PickedStatus],
			[PickedDt],
			[ActualStartDt],
			[ActualEndDt],
			[DependSysLandscape],
			[DependTaskID],
			[CreatedBy],
			[CreatedDt],
			[ModifiedBy],
			[ModifiedDt]
			)
			VALUES (
			@ITCRID,
			@SysLandscape,
			@ExecutionStepName,
			@ExecutionStepDesc,
			@AssignedTo,
			@StartDt,
			@EndDT,
			@Attachments,
			@Status,
			@ForwardStatus,
			@ForwardedTo,
			@ForwardedDt,
			@ReasonForwarded,
			@Remarks,
			@PickedStatus,
			@PickedDt,
			@ActualStartDt,
			@ActualEndDt,
			@DependSysLandscape,
			@DependTaskID,
			@CreatedBy,
			getdate(),
			@CreatedBy,
			getdate()
			)
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[CRExecutionPlan] SET
				[ITCRID]=@ITCRID,
				[SysLandscape]=@SysLandscape,
				[ExecutionStepName]=@ExecutionStepName,
				[ExecutionStepDesc]=@ExecutionStepDesc,
				[AssignedTo]=@AssignedTo,
				[StartDt]=@StartDt,
				[EndDT]=@EndDT,
				[Attachments]=@Attachments,
				[Status]=@Status,
				[ForwardStatus]=@ForwardStatus,
				[ForwardedTo]=@ForwardedTo,
				[ForwardedDt]=@ForwardedDt,
				[ReasonForwarded]=@ReasonForwarded,
			    [Remarks]=@Remarks,
			    [PickedStatus]=@PickedStatus,
				[PickedDt]=@PickedDt,
				[ActualStartDt]=@ActualStartDt,
				[ActualEndDt]=@ActualEndDt,
				[DependSysLandscape]=@DependSysLandscape,
				[DependTaskID]=@DependTaskID,
				[ModifiedBy]=@CreatedBy,
				[ModifiedDt]=getdate()
			WHERE ITCRExecID=@ITCRExecID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete CR Approver Field
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			DELETE FROM [IT].[CRExecutionPlan] WHERE ITCRExecID=@ITCRExecID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='V'   -- Delete CR Approver Field
	BEGIN
		SELECT * FROM [IT].[CRExecutionPlan] WHERE ITCRID=@ITCRID AND SysLandscape=@SysLandscape
		
	END
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()

	
	IF @Status='Implemented'
	Begin
	  Begin transaction
		update it.changerequest set Stage='Implementation', Status='Implemented', isImplemented=1, Remarks=@Remarks, ModifiedBy=@CreatedBy,
				ModifiedDt=getdate() where ITCRID=@ITCRID

		Update IT.CRMilestone Set ImplementedDt=getdate() where ITCRID=@ITCRID
		
	  commit transaction
	End
	Else
	Begin
	  Begin transaction
		update it.changerequest set Stage='Implementation', Status='Implement', Remarks=@Remarks, ModifiedBy=@CreatedBy,
				ModifiedDt=getdate() where ITCRID=@ITCRID
	  commit transaction
	End
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('CRExecutionPlan Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END
GO

-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_CRFollowup](
	@Flag [char](1),
	@CRFollowupID [int] NULL,
	@ITCRID [int],
	@FollowupDt [datetime] NULL,
	@FollowupToPerson [int] NULL,
	@FollowupComments [nvarchar](max),
	@CreatedBy [int] NULL
	
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert CR Release Fields
	BEGIN 
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
				
			INSERT INTO [IT].[CRFollowup] (
				[ITCRID],
				[FollowupDt],
				[FollowupToPerson],
				[FollowupComments] ,
				[CreatedBy] ,
				[CreatedDt])
			VALUES (
				@ITCRID,
				@FollowupDt,
				@FollowupToPerson,
				@FollowupComments,
				@CreatedBy,
				getdate()
				)
		COMMIT TRANSACTION

		 Begin transaction
		update it.changerequest set Remarks=@FollowupComments, ModifiedBy=@CreatedBy,
				ModifiedDt=getdate() where ITCRID=@ITCRID
	  commit transaction
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[CRFollowup] SET
				[ITCRID]=@ITCRID,
				[FollowupDt]=@FollowupDT,
				[FollowupToPerson]=@FollowupToPerson,
				[FollowupComments]=@FollowupComments,
				[ModifiedBy]=@CreatedBy,
				[ModifiedDt]=getdate()
			WHERE CRFollowupID=@CRFollowupID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION

		 Begin transaction
		update it.changerequest set Remarks=@FollowupComments, ModifiedBy=@CreatedBy,
				ModifiedDt=getdate() where ITCRID=@ITCRID
	  commit transaction
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete CR Approver Field
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			DELETE FROM [IT].[CRFollowup] WHERE CRFollowupID=@CRFollowupID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('CRLession Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END

CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_CRRefrence](
	@Flag [char](1),
	@ReferenceID [int] NULL,
	@ReferenceName char(10) NULL,
	@IsActive bit NULL,
	@CreatedBy int NULL,
	@CreatedDate datetime NULL,
	@ModifiedBy int NULL,
	@ModifiedDate datetime NULL
	
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert CR Release Fields
	BEGIN 
		BEGIN TRANSACTION

		
			INSERT INTO [IT].[Reference] (
			[ReferenceName],
			[IsActive],
			[CreatedBy],
			[CreatedDate]
		 )
			VALUES (
			@ReferenceName,
			@IsActive,
			@CreatedBy,
			getdate()
			)
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[Reference] SET
				[ReferenceName]=@ReferenceName,
				[IsActive]=@IsActive,
				[ModifiedBy]=@ModifiedBy,
				[ModifiedDate]=getdate()
			WHERE ReferenceID=@ReferenceID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete CR Approver Field

		BEGIN TRANSACTION

		COMMIT TRANSACTION

BEGIN CATCH

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_CRRelease]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_CRRelease](
	@Flag [char](1),
	@CRReleaseID [int] NULL,
	@ITCRID [int],
	@SysLandscape [int],
	@ReleaseComments [nvarchar](MAX),
	@AssignedTo [int] NULL,
	@ReleaseDt [datetime] NULL,
	@Attachments [nchar](50) NULL,
	@Status [nchar](10) NULL,
	@ApprovedBy [int] NULL,
	@ApprovedDt [datetime] NULL,
	@CreatedBy [int] NULL
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Declare @Stage char(1), @level int
	select @Stage='R'

	IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert CR Release Fields
	BEGIN 
		BEGIN TRANSACTION

		
			INSERT INTO [IT].[CRRelease] (
			[ITCRID],
			[SysLandscape],
			[ReleaseComments],
			[AssignedTo],
			[ReleaseDt],
			[Attachments],
			[Status],
			[ApprovedBy],
			[ApprovedDt],
			[CreatedBy],
			[CreatedDt]
			)
			VALUES (
			@ITCRID,
			@SysLandscape,
			@ReleaseComments,
			@AssignedTo,
			@ReleaseDt,
			@Attachments,
			@Status,
			@ApprovedBy,
			@ApprovedDt,
			@CreatedBy,
			getdate()
			)
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[CRRelease] SET
				[Status]=@Status,
				[ModifiedBy]=@CreatedBy,
				[ModifiedDt]=getdate()
			WHERE CRReleaseID=@CRReleaseID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete CR Approver Field
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			DELETE FROM [IT].[CRRelease] WHERE CRReleaseID=@CRReleaseID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()
	
	select @level = max(level) from it.Approver app
	inner join it.ChangeRequest cr on cr.CategoryID=app.CategoryID and cr.ClassifcationID=app.ClassificationID
	where cr.ITCRID=@ITCRID and app.Approverstage=@Stage

	IF @Stage ='R'
	BEGIN
		BEGIN transaction
			update it.ChangeRequest set isReleased=1 , Stage='Release', Status='Released', Remarks=@ReleaseComments, ModifiedBy=@CreatedBy,
				ModifiedDt=getdate() where ITCRID=@ITCRID

			update IT.CRMilestone set  ReleasedBy=@CreatedBy, ReleasedDt=getdate() where ITCRID=@ITCRID
		commit transaction
	END
		
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('CRRelease Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_CRTaskEmail]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
Create PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_CRTaskEmail](
	@CRID [int]  NULL
	
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	
select CR.ITCRID, CR.CRCode,CR.SupportID
,isNull(suppt.First_Name,'')+' '+isNull(suppt.Middle_Name,'')+' '+isNull(suppt.Last_Name,'') CROwner, suppt.Email CROEmail, suppt.Designation CRODesignation,suppt.Role CRORole,suppt.EmpID CROEmpid
,isNull(supptI.First_Name,'')+' '+isNull(supptI.Middle_Name,'')+' '+isNull(supptI.Last_Name,'') CRInitiator, supptI.Email CRIEmail, supptI.Designation CRIDesignation,supptI.Role CRIRole, supptI.EmpID CRIEmpid
,isNull(supptR.First_Name,'')+' '+isNull(supptR.Middle_Name,'')+' '+isNull(supptR.Last_Name,'') CRRequestor, supptR.Email CRREmail, supptR.Designation CRRDesignation,supptR.Role CRRRole, supptR.EmpID CRREmpid
,CR.ChangeDesc, Cat.ITCategoryID, Cat.CategoryName, Class.ITClassificationID, CR.PlantID as plantcode
,Class.ClassificationName,CR.CRDate,CR.Stage, CR.[Status], CR.ApprovedBy
,execp.ITCRExecID TaskID, execp.ExecutionStepName TaskName, execp.ExecutionStepDesc TaskDesc
,execp.AssignedTo AssignedTo, isNull(supptAssgn.First_Name,'')+' '+isNull(supptAssgn.Middle_Name,'')+' '+isNull(supptAssgn.Last_Name,'') AssignedToName, supptAssgn.Email AssgnEmail, supptAssgn.Designation AssgnDesignation,supptAssgn.Role AssgnRole,supptAssgn.EmpID AssgnEmpid
,execp.ForwardedTo, isNull(supptFwd.First_Name,'')+' '+isNull(supptFwd.Middle_Name,'')+' '+isNull(supptFwd.Last_Name,'') ForwardToName, supptFwd.Email ForwardToEmail, supptFwd.Designation ForwardToDesignation,supptFwd.Role ForwardToRole,supptFwd.EmpID ForwardToEmpid
,execp.Status EStatus, execp.PickedDt,execp.PickedStatus,  execp.ModifiedDt AssignedDt

		from IT.ChangeRequest as CR
		inner join  IT.Category Cat on cat.ITCategoryID=cr.CategoryID 
		inner join IT.Classification Class on Class.ITClassificationID=CR.ClassifcationID
		inner join IT.CategoryTyp catTyp on catTyp.CategoryID=CR.CategoryTypeID
		inner join Plant_Master plant on plant.Id = CR.PlantID
		inner join IT.CRExecutionPlan execp on execp.ITCRID=CR.ITCRID
		inner join IT.SupportTeam suppt on suppt.EmpID=CR.CROwner
		inner join IT.SupportTeam supptI on supptI.EmpID=CR.CRInitiatedFor
		inner join IT.SupportTeam supptR on supptR.EmpID=CR.CRRequestedBy
		Left join IT.SupportTeam supptAssgn on supptAssgn.EmpID=execp.AssignedTo
		Left join IT.SupportTeam supptFwd on supptFwd.EmpID=execp.ForwardedTo
		where CR.ITCRID=@CRID

END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('Category Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_CRTemplate]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_CRTemplate](
	@Flag Char(1),
	 @CRTemplateID int NULL
	 ,@TemplateName varchar(500)
	 ,@CRID int
	,@CRTemplateDtlsID int NULL
	,@SupportID int 
    ,@SysLandscapeID int NULL
	,@ClassificationID int
    ,@CategoryID int
    ,@CategoryTypID int
    ,@TaskName varchar(500) NULL
    ,@TaskDesc varchar(2000) NULL
    ,@Priority int NULL
    ,@IsActive bit
    ,@CreatedBy int 
	)
AS
BEGIN 
Declare @count int=0

BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	
	Select @count=count(CRTemplateID) from IT.CRTemplate where TemplateName=@TemplateName and CategoryID=@CategoryID and CategoryTypID=  @CategoryTypID

	if (@count>1) return

	IF (@count=0)
	BEGIN 
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
	--	Print 'Inside'
			INSERT INTO [IT].[CRTemplate]
           ([SupportID]
           ,[CategoryID]
           ,[CategoryTypID]
           ,[TemplateName]
           ,[IsActive]
           ,[CreatedBy]
           ,[CreatedDt]
           ,[ModifiedBy]
           ,[ModifiedDt])
			 VALUES
           (@SupportID
           ,@CategoryID
           ,@CategoryTypID
           ,@TemplateName
           ,@IsActive
           ,@CreatedBy
           ,getdate()
           ,@CreatedBy
           ,getdate())


			IF (@@ERROR<>'')
			BEGIN
				ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
				RETURN error_message()
			END
			COMMIT TRANSACTION
		
		--Insert into CR TEMPLATE DETAILS--
		Select @CRTemplateID=CRTemplateID from IT.CRTemplate where TemplateName=@TemplateName

		BEGIN TRANSACTION
		INSERT INTO [IT].[CRTemplateDtls]
				   ([CRTemplateID]
				   ,[SysLandscapeID]
				   ,[CategoryID]
				   ,[CategoryTypID]
				   ,[TaskName]
				   ,[TaskDesc]
				   ,[Priority]
				   ,[IsActive]
				   ,[CreatedBy]
				   ,[CreatedDt]
				   ,[ModifiedBy]
				   ,[ModifiedDt])
			 Select
				   @CRTemplateID
				   ,sysl.SysLandscapeID
				   ,@CategoryID
				   ,@CategoryTypID
				   ,CRE.ExecutionStepName
				   ,CRE.ExecutionStepDesc
				   ,sysl.PriorityNum
				   ,@IsActive
				   ,@CreatedBy
				   ,getdate()
				   ,@CreatedBy
				   ,getdate() from IT.CRExecutionPlan CRE 
				   inner join IT.SysLandscape sysl on sysl.SysLandscapeID=CRE.SysLandscape
				   where CRE.ITCRID=@CRID

		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete CR Approver Field
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()

	 
	
	END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_CRTemplateExecPlan]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_CRTemplateExecPlan](
	@Flag Char(1)
	,@CRTemplateID int
	,@CRID int
	,@CreatedBy int 
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Declare @count int=0
	Select @count=count(ITCRID) from IT.CRExecutionPlan where ITCRID=@CRID

	
	IF (@count=0)
	BEGIN 
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
		--Print 'Inside'
	
		INSERT INTO [IT].[CRExecutionPlan]
			   ([ITCRID]
			   ,[SysLandscape]
			   ,[ExecutionStepName]
			   ,[ExecutionStepDesc]
			   ,[CreatedBy]
			   ,[CreatedDt]
			   ,[ModifiedBy]
			   ,[ModifiedDt])
			  
		Select
				@CRID	  
				,tmpl.SysLandscapeID
				,tmpl.TaskName
				,tmpl.TaskDesc
				,@CreatedBy
				,getdate()
				,@CreatedBy
				,getdate()
				 from  [IT].[CRTemplateDtls]  tmpl
				where tmpl.CRTemplateID=@CRTemplateID

				IF (@@ERROR<>'')
				Begin
					ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
					return
				End
				
			COMMIT TRANSACTION
		END


	Select @count=count(ITCRID) from IT.CRExecutionPlan where ITCRID=@CRID
		
	
	If (@count>0)
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION

			UPDATE IT.ChangeRequest set Stage='Implementation', [Status]='Implement', ModifiedBy=@CreatedBy, ModifiedDt=getdate() where ITCRID=@CRID
		
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
		
	END
	

	END TRY
	
	BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
	END CATCH
END

GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_GetApprover]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_GetApprover](
	@Level [int],
	@stage [char](1) ,
	@plantid [int],
	@categoryid [int],
	@classificationid[int])
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	select apv.ITApproverID, @stage stage,
	apv.Approver1,concat(sta1.First_Name,'',sta1.Middle_Name,' ',sta1.Last_Name,' (',sta1.EmpID,')')  Approver1Name,
	apv.Approver2,concat(sta2.First_Name,'',sta2.Middle_Name ,' ',sta2.Last_Name,' (',sta2.EmpID,')') Approver2Name,
	apv.Approver3,concat(sta3.First_Name,'',sta3.Middle_Name ,' ',sta3.Last_Name,' (',sta3.EmpID,')') Approver3Name,
	(select (count(Level)) from [IT].[Approver] where Approverstage=@stage and plantid=@plantid and CategoryID=@categoryid and ClassificationID=@classificationid and SupportID=1) as ApproverCount
	from IT.Approver apv
	inner join IT.SupportTeam sta1 on sta1.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver1 
	LEFT join IT.SupportTeam sta2 on sta2.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver2 
	Left join IT.SupportTeam sta3 on sta3.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver3 
	where apv.SupportID=1 and apv.Level=@Level and apv.Approverstage=@stage and plantid=@plantid and apv.ClassificationID=@classificationid and apv.CategoryID=@categoryid

	return
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_GetApproverforEmail]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_GetApproverforEmail](
	@stage [char](1) ,
	@plantid [int],
	@categoryid [int],
	@classificationid[int])
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	select apv.level,apv.approverstage
	,apv.Approver1,concat(sta1.First_Name,'',sta1.Middle_Name,' ',sta1.Last_Name) Approver1Name,sta1.EmpID EmpID1,sta1.Email Approver1Email
	,apv.Approver2,concat(sta2.First_Name,'',sta2.Middle_Name ,' ',sta2.Last_Name) Approver2Name,sta2.EmpID EmpID2,sta2.Email Approver2Email
	,apv.Approver3,concat(sta3.First_Name,'',sta3.Middle_Name ,' ',sta3.Last_Name) Approver3Name,sta3.EmpID EmpID3,sta3.Email Approver3Email
	from IT.Approver apv
	inner join IT.SupportTeam sta1 on sta1.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver1 
	LEFT join IT.SupportTeam sta2 on sta2.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver2 
	Left join IT.SupportTeam sta3 on sta3.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver3 
	where apv.SupportID=1 and plantid=@plantid and apv.ClassificationID=@classificationid and apv.CategoryID=@categoryid and APV.LEVEL=1 and apv.approverstage=@stage
	Union All
	select apv.level,apv.approverstage
	,apv.Approver1,concat(sta1.First_Name,'',sta1.Middle_Name,' ',sta1.Last_Name) Approver1Name,sta1.EmpID EmpID1,sta1.Email Approver1Email
	,apv.Approver2,concat(sta2.First_Name,'',sta2.Middle_Name ,' ',sta2.Last_Name) Approver2Name,sta2.EmpID EmpID2,sta2.Email Approver2Email
	,apv.Approver3,concat(sta3.First_Name,'',sta3.Middle_Name ,' ',sta3.Last_Name) Approver3Name,sta3.EmpID EmpID3,sta3.Email Approver3Email
	from IT.Approver apv
	inner join IT.SupportTeam sta1 on sta1.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver1 
	LEFT join IT.SupportTeam sta2 on sta2.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver2 
	Left join IT.SupportTeam sta3 on sta3.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver3 
	where apv.SupportID=1 and plantid=@plantid and apv.ClassificationID=@classificationid and apv.CategoryID=@categoryid and APV.LEVEL=2 and apv.approverstage=@stage
	Union All
	select apv.level,apv.approverstage
	,apv.Approver1,concat(sta1.First_Name,'',sta1.Middle_Name,' ',sta1.Last_Name) Approver1Name,sta1.EmpID EmpID1,sta1.Email Approver1Email
	,apv.Approver2,concat(sta2.First_Name,'',sta2.Middle_Name ,' ',sta2.Last_Name) Approver2Name,sta2.EmpID EmpID2,sta2.Email Approver2Email
	,apv.Approver3,concat(sta3.First_Name,'',sta3.Middle_Name ,' ',sta3.Last_Name) Approver3Name,sta3.EmpID EmpID3,sta3.Email Approver3Email
	from IT.Approver apv
	inner join IT.SupportTeam sta1 on sta1.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver1 
	LEFT join IT.SupportTeam sta2 on sta2.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver2 
	Left join IT.SupportTeam sta3 on sta3.SupportTeamID=apv.Approver3 
	where apv.SupportID=1 and plantid=@plantid and apv.ClassificationID=@classificationid and apv.CategoryID=@categoryid and APV.LEVEL=3 and apv.approverstage=@stage

	return
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END

CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_GetCRHistory](

)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from

	CR.PlantID,
	CR.GXPClassification,

	CR.ReasonForChange,
	CR.AlternateConsidetation,
	CR.ImpactNotDoing,
	CR.BusinessImpact,
	CR.TriggeredBy,
	CR.Benefits,
	CR.EstimatedCost,
	CR.EstimatedCostCurr,

	CR.ApprovedDt,
	CR.isSubmitted,
	CR.isApproved,

	CR.isReleased,

	CR.ClosedBy,

-- =============================================

CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_IssueAssigned](
	@Flag [char](1),
	@IssueID [int] NULL,
	@AssignedTo [int] NULL,
	@AssignedBy [int] NULL,
	@Status [varchar](50) NULL
	--@CreatedBy [int] NULL,
	--@CreatedDt [datetime] NULL
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[IssueList] SET
				[AssignedTo]=@AssignedTo,
				[AssignedBy]=@AssignedBy,
				[AssignedOn]=getdate(),
				[ModifiedBy]=@AssignedBy,
				[ModifiedDt]=getdate(),
				[Status]=@Status
			WHERE IssueID=@IssueID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN

			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('IssueList Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_IssueList]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO





-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_IssueList](
	@Flag [char](1),
	@IssueID [int] NULL Output, 
	@IssueSelectedfor [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@IssueRaisedBy [int] NULL,
	@IssueDate [datetime],
	@IssueShotDesc [nvarchar](200),
	@IssueDesc [nvarchar](Max),
	@IssueRaiseFor [int] NULL,
	@IssueForGuest [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@GuestEmployeeId [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@GuestName [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@GuestEmail [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@GuestContactNo [varchar](20) NULL,
	@GuestReportingManagerEmployeeId [nvarchar](200) NULL,
    @Type [nvarchar](50) NULL,
	@GuestCompany [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@PlantID [int] NULL,
	@AssetID [int] NULL,
	@CategoryID [int] NULL,
	@CategoryTypID [int] NULL,
	@Priority [int] NULL,
	@Source [nvarchar](100) NULL,
	@Attachment [nvarchar](100) NULL,
	@Status [nchar](50) NULL,
	@AssignedTo [int] NULL,
	@AssignedBy [int] NULL,
	@AssignedOn [datetime] NULL,
	@Remarks [nvarchar](3000) NULL,
	@ProposedResolutionOn [datetime] NULL,
	@ResolutionDt [datetime] NULL,
	@ReasonID [int] NULL,
	@CreatedBy [int] NULL,
	@CreatedDt [datetime] NULL,
	@ModifiedBy [int] NULL,
	@ModifiedDt [datetime] NULL
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

Declare
@PlantCode  varchar(6),
@IssueCode varchar(20),
@MaxCount varchar(4),
@Year varchar(4),
@return_value varchar(20),
@err_num int,
@err_msg varchar(100)

	IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert CR Release Fields
	BEGIN 
		select @PlantCode= PlantCode from IT.Plant_Master where PlantID=@PlantID
		select @MaxCount = count(IssueID)+1 from [IT].[IssueList]
		select @Year=DATEPART(year, getdate())
	    select @IssueCode= CONCAT (@PlantCode,'/IS/',@Year,'/',@MaxCount)
		BEGIN TRANSACTION

			
			INSERT INTO [IT].[IssueList] (
			[IssueCode],
			[IssueSelectedfor],
			[IssueRaisedBy],
			[IssueDate],
			[IssueShotDesc],
			[IssueDesc],
			[IssueRaiseFor],
			[IssueForGuest],
			[GuestEmployeeId],
			[GuestName],
			[GuestEmail],
			[GuestContactNo],
			[GuestReportingManagerEmployeeId],
			[Type],
			[GuestCompany],
			[PlantID],
			[AssetID],
			[CategoryID],
			[CategoryTypID],
			[Priority],
			[Source],
			[Attachment],
			[Status],
			[AssignedTo],
			[AssignedBy],
			[AssignedOn],
			[Remarks],
			[ProposedResolutionOn],
			[ReasonID],
			[CreatedBy],
			[CreatedDt],
			[ModifiedBy],
			[ModifiedDt]
			
		 )
			VALUES (
			ltrim(rtrim(@IssueCode)),
			@IssueSelectedfor,
			@IssueRaisedBy,
			getdate(),
			@IssueShotDesc,
			@IssueDesc,
			@IssueRaiseFor,
			@IssueForGuest,
			@GuestEmployeeId,
			@GuestName,
			@GuestEmail,
			@GuestContactNo,
			@GuestReportingManagerEmployeeId,
			@Type,
			@GuestCompany,
			@PlantID,
			@AssetID,
			@CategoryID,
			@CategoryTypID,
			@Priority,
			@Source,
			@Attachment,
			@Status,
			@AssignedTo,
			@AssignedBy,
			getdate(),
			@Remarks,
			@ProposedResolutionOn,
			@ReasonID,
			@CreatedBy,
			getdate(),
			@ModifiedBy,
			getdate()
			
			)
			SET @IssueID = SCOPE_IDENTITY();
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
		
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[IssueList] SET
				[IssueRaisedBy]=@IssueRaisedBy,
				[IssueDate]=getdate(),
				[IssueShotDesc]=@IssueShotDesc,
				[IssueDesc]=@IssueDesc,
				[IssueRaiseFor]=@IssueRaiseFor,
				[IssueSelectedfor]=@IssueSelectedfor,
				[IssueForGuest]=@IssueForGuest,
				[GuestCompany]=@GuestCompany,
				[GuestEmployeeId]=@GuestEmployeeId,
				[GuestName]=@GuestName,
				[GuestEmail]=@GuestEmail,
				[GuestContactNo]=@GuestContactNo,
				[GuestReportingManagerEmployeeId]=@GuestReportingManagerEmployeeId,
				[Type]=@Type,
				[PlantID]=@PlantID,
				[AssetID]=@AssetID,
				[CategoryID]=@CategoryID,
				[AssignedTo]=@AssignedTo,
				[AssignedBy]=@AssignedBy,
				[AssignedOn]=@AssignedOn,
				[CategoryTypID]=@CategoryTypID,
				[Priority]=@Priority,
				[Source]=@Source,
				[Attachment]=@Attachment,
				[Status]=@Status,
				[Remarks]=@Remarks,
				[ProposedResolutionOn]=@ProposedResolutionOn,
				[ResolutionDt]=@ResolutionDt,
				[ReasonID] = @ReasonID,
				[ModifiedBy]=@CreatedBy,
				[ModifiedDt]=getdate()
				
			WHERE IssueID=@IssueID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete CR Approver Field
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			DELETE FROM [IT].[IssueList] WHERE IssueID=@IssueID
		
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('IssueList Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END
GO

BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_ITAssets](
	@Flag Char(1),
	@ITAssetID [int] NULL,
	@Requesttype [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@RequestedBY [int] NULL,
	@RequestedFor [int] NULL,
	@SelectedFor [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@PlantID [int] NULL,
	@SupportID [int] NULL,
	@EmpType [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@Guest_Id [int] NULL,
	@Guest_Name [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Guest_Email [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Guest_RManagerId [int] NULL,
	@Guest_ContactNo [int] NULL,
	@Assettype [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Emp_Id [int] NULL,
	@GxpReq [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@ExistingAsset [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@AssetModel [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@AssetSerialNo [nvarchar](300) NULL,
	@AssetsWarranty_EndDt [datetime] NULL,
	@SuggModel [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@Specs_Requirements [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@ApproximateINR [int] NULL,
	@Justification [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@HOD_Approval [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@IsActive [bit] NULL,
	@Status [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@CreatedBy [int] NULL
	)
	
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	
	DECLARE @level int=0,
	@PlantCode  varchar(6),
	@AssetCode varchar(20),
	@MaxCount varchar(4),
	@Year varchar(4),
	@return_value varchar(20)

	IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert SLA Fields
	BEGIN 
		select @PlantCode= PlantCode from IT.Plant_Master where PlantID=@PlantID
		select @MaxCount = count(ITAssetID)+1 from [IT].[ITAssetDetails]
		select @Year=DATEPART(year, getdate())
	    select @AssetCode= CONCAT (@PlantCode,'/AS/',@Year,'/',@MaxCount)
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			INSERT INTO [IT].[ITAssetDetails]
           (  [AssetCode]
		      ,[Requesttype]
			  ,[RequestedBY]
			  ,[RequestedFor]
			  ,[SelectedFor]
			  ,[EmpType]
			  ,[Guest_Id]
			  ,[Guest_Name]
			  ,[Guest_Email]
			  ,[Guest_RManagerId]
			  ,[Guest_ContactNo]
			  ,[Assettype]
			  ,[Emp_Id]
			  ,[SupportID]
			  ,[GxpReq]
			  ,[ExistingAsset]
			  ,[AssetModel]
			  ,[AssetSerialNo]
			  ,[AssetsWarranty_EndDt]
			  ,[SuggModel]
			  ,[Specs_Requirements]
			  ,[ApproximateINR]
			  ,[Justification]
			  ,[HOD_Approval]
			  ,[IsActive]
			  ,[Status]
			  ,[CreatedBy]
			  ,[CreatedDt]
			  ,[ModifiedBy]
			  ,[ModifiedDt]

			)
     VALUES
           (ltrim(rtrim(@AssetCode)) 
		    ,@Requesttype
			,@RequestedBY
			,@RequestedFor
			,@SelectedFor
			,@EmpType
			,@Guest_Id
			,@Guest_Name
			,@Guest_Email
			,@Guest_RManagerId
			,@Guest_ContactNo
			,@Assettype
			,@Emp_Id
			,@SupportID
			,@GxpReq
			,@ExistingAsset
			,@AssetModel
			,@AssetSerialNo
			,@AssetsWarranty_EndDt
			,@SuggModel
			,@Specs_Requirements
			,@ApproximateINR
			,@Justification
			,@HOD_Approval
			,@IsActive
			,@Status
			,@CreatedBy
			,getdate()
			,@CreatedBy
			,getdate()
			)
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update SLA Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[ITAssetDetails] SET
			[Requesttype] =@Requesttype
			,[RequestedBY] =@RequestedBY
			,[RequestedFor] =@RequestedFor
			,[SelectedFor] = @SelectedFor
			,[EmpType] =@EmpType
			,[SupportID] =@SupportID
			,[Guest_Id] = @Guest_Id
			,[Guest_Name] = @Guest_Name
			,[Guest_Email] =@Guest_Email
			,[Guest_RManagerId] = @Guest_RManagerId
			,[Guest_ContactNo] = @Guest_ContactNo
			,[Assettype] = @Assettype
			,[Emp_Id] = @Emp_Id
			,[GxpReq] = @GxpReq
			,[ExistingAsset] = @ExistingAsset
			,[AssetModel] = @AssetModel
			,[AssetSerialNo] = @AssetSerialNo
			,[AssetsWarranty_EndDt] = @AssetsWarranty_EndDt
			,[SuggModel] = @SuggModel
			,[Specs_Requirements] = @Specs_Requirements
			,[ApproximateINR] = @ApproximateINR
			,[Justification] =@Justification
			,[HOD_Approval]=@HOD_Approval
			,[IsActive] = @IsActive
			,[Status] = @Status
			,[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy
			,[ModifiedDt] =GETDATE()
		
			WHERE ITAssetID=@ITAssetID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete SLA Field
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			DELETE FROM [IT].[ITAssetDetails] WHERE ITAssetID=@ITAssetID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()

	END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_ITSpare](
	@Flag Char(1),
	@ITSpareID [int] NULL,
	@SupportID [int] NULL,
	@Requesttype [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@PlantID [int] NULL,
	@RequestedBY [int] NULL,
	@RequestedFor [int] NULL,
	@SelectedFor [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Guest_Id [int] NULL,
	@Guest_Name [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Guest_Email [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Guest_RManagerId [int] NULL,
	@Guest_ContactNo [int] NULL,
	@EmpType [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@Emp_Id [int] NULL,
	@GxpReq [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@Asset_Type [nvarchar](300) NULL,
	@Spare_Type [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Spare_Model [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Spare_SerialNo [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Specs_Requirements [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Specification [nvarchar](max) NULL,
	@Justification [nvarchar](200) NULL,
	@HOD_Approval [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Status [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@IsActive [bit] NULL,
	@CreatedBy [int] NULL
	)
	
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	DECLARE @level int=0,
	@PlantCode  varchar(6),
	@SpareCode varchar(20),
	@MaxCount varchar(4),
	@Year varchar(4),
	@return_value varchar(20)

	IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert SLA Fields
	BEGIN 
		select @PlantCode= PlantCode from IT.Plant_Master where PlantID=@PlantID
		select @MaxCount = count(ITSpareID)+1 from [IT].[ITSpare]
		select @Year=DATEPART(year, getdate())
	    select @SpareCode= CONCAT (@PlantCode,'/AS/',@Year,'/',@MaxCount)
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			INSERT INTO [IT].[ITSpare]
           (
		   [ITSpareCode]
		   ,[Requesttype]
		   ,[SupportID]
		  ,[RequestedBY]
		  ,[RequestedFor]
		  ,[SelectedFor]
		  ,[Guest_Id]
		  ,[Guest_Name]
		  ,[Guest_Email]
		  ,[Guest_RManagerId]
		  ,[Guest_ContactNo]
		  ,[EmpType]
		  ,[Emp_Id]
		  ,[GxpReq]
		  ,[Asset_Type]
		  ,[Spare_Type]
		  ,[Spare_Model]
		  ,[Spare_SerialNo]
		  ,[Specs_Requirements]
		  ,[Specification]
		  ,[Justification]
		  ,[HOD_Approval]
		  ,[IsActive]
		  ,[Status]
		  ,[CreatedBy]
		  ,[CreatedDt]
		  ,[ModifiedBy]
		  ,[ModifiedDt]
			)
     VALUES
		   (ltrim(rtrim(@SpareCode)) 
			,@Requesttype
			,@SupportID
			,@RequestedBY
			,@RequestedFor
			,@SelectedFor
			,@Guest_Id
			,@Guest_Name
			,@Guest_Email
			,@Guest_RManagerId
			,@Guest_ContactNo
			,@EmpType
			,@Emp_Id
			,@GxpReq
			,@Asset_Type
			,@Spare_Type
			,@Spare_Model
			,@Spare_SerialNo
			,@Specs_Requirements
			,@Specification
	  		,@Justification
			,@HOD_Approval
			,@IsActive
			,@Status
			,@CreatedBy
			,GETDATE()
			,@CreatedBy
			,getdate()
			)
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update SLA Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[ITSpare] SET
			[Requesttype] = @Requesttype
			,[SupportID] = @SupportID
			,[RequestedBY] = @RequestedBY
			,[RequestedFor] =@RequestedFor
			,[SelectedFor] = @SelectedFor
			,[Guest_Id] = @Guest_Id
			,[Guest_Name] = @Guest_Name
			,[Guest_Email] = @Guest_Email
			,[Guest_RManagerId] = @Guest_RManagerId
			,[Guest_ContactNo] = @Guest_ContactNo
			,[EmpType] = @EmpType
			,[Emp_Id] = @Emp_Id
			,[GxpReq] = @GxpReq
			,[Asset_Type] = @Asset_Type
			,[Spare_Type] =@Spare_Type
			,[Spare_Model] = @Spare_Model
			,[Spare_SerialNo] = @Spare_SerialNo
			,[Specs_Requirements] = @Specs_Requirements
			,[Specification] = @Specification
			,[Justification] = @Justification
			,[HOD_Approval] = @HOD_Approval
			,[IsActive] = @IsActive
			,[Status] =@Status
			,[ModifiedBy] =@CreatedBy
			,[ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
		
			WHERE ITSpareID=@ITSpareID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete SLA Field
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			DELETE FROM [IT].[ITSpare] WHERE ITSpareID=@ITSpareID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()

	END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_ManageProjectChecklist]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_ManageProjectChecklist]
    @Flag CHAR(1),              
    @checkListId INT = NULL,
    @checkListTital NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @TaskId INT = NULL,         
    @ProjectMgmtID INT = NULL,  
    @SubTaskId INT = NULL,      
    @MileStoneId INT = NULL,    
    @ProjectLevel NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @Description NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @CreatedBy INT = NULL,
    @CreatedDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @ModifiedBy INT = NULL,
    @ModifiedDt DATETIME = NULL
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    IF @Flag = 'I'
    BEGIN
        INSERT INTO IT.ProjectCheckList (
            checkListTitle,TaskId, ProjectMgmtID, SubTaskId, MileStoneId, ProjectLevel, 
            Description,CreatedBy, CreatedDt, ModifiedBy, ModifiedDt
        )
        VALUES (
            @checkListTital,@TaskId, @ProjectMgmtID, @SubTaskId, @MileStoneId, @ProjectLevel,
            @Description,@CreatedBy, ISNULL(@CreatedDt, GETDATE()), 
            @ModifiedBy, GETDATE()
        );
		UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
		SET
		[Activity] = 'Project CheckList Created',
		[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
        [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
		where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID
    END

    IF @Flag = 'U'
    BEGIN
        IF @checkListId IS NOT NULL
        BEGIN
            UPDATE IT.ProjectCheckList
            SET 
                checkListTitle = COALESCE(NULLIF(@checkListTital, ''), ProjectLevel),
                TaskId = COALESCE(NULLIF(@TaskId, NULL), TaskId),
                ProjectMgmtID = COALESCE(NULLIF(@ProjectMgmtID, NULL), ProjectMgmtID),
                SubTaskId = COALESCE(NULLIF(@SubTaskId, NULL), SubTaskId),
                MileStoneId = COALESCE(NULLIF(@MileStoneId, NULL), MileStoneId),
                ProjectLevel = COALESCE(NULLIF(@ProjectLevel, ''), ProjectLevel),
                Description = COALESCE(NULLIF(@Description, ''), Description),
                ModifiedBy = COALESCE(NULLIF(@ModifiedBy, NULL), ModifiedBy),
                ModifiedDt = GETDATE()
            WHERE checkListId = @checkListId;
			UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
		SET
		[Activity] = 'Project CheckList Updated',
		[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
        [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
		where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('issueId is required for update operation', 16, 1);
        END
    END

    IF @Flag = 'D'
    BEGIN
        IF @checkListId IS NOT NULL
        BEGIN
            DELETE FROM IT.ProjectCheckList
            WHERE checkListId = @checkListId;
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('checkList Id is required for delete operation', 16, 1);
        END
    END
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_ManageProjectIssue]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_ManageProjectIssue]
    @Flag CHAR(1),              -- 'I' for Insert, 'U' for Update, 'D' for Delete
    @issueId INT = NULL,        -- issueId for Update or Delete
    @TaskId INT = NULL,         
    @ProjectMgmtID INT = NULL,  
    @SubTaskId INT = NULL,      
    @MileStoneId INT = NULL,    
    @ProjectLevel NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @Description NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @Priority NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @Impact NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @DateOpened DATETIME = NULL,
    @DateClosed DATETIME = NULL,
    @IssueOwner INT = NULL,
    @Department NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @Status NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @Notes NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @AssignedTo INT = NULL,
    @AssignedBy INT = NULL,
    @AssignedOn DATETIME = NULL,
    @CreatedBy INT = NULL,
    @CreatedDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @ModifiedBy INT = NULL,
    @ModifiedDt DATETIME = NULL
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert Operation (I)
    IF @Flag = 'I'
    BEGIN
	
        DECLARE @IssueCode NVARCHAR(200);
	 DECLARE @IssueCount INT;
        SELECT @IssueCount = COUNT(*) 
        FROM IT.ProjectIssue
        WHERE ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID AND MileStoneId = @MileStoneId AND TaskId = @TaskId;

        SET @IssueCode = 'PR' + CAST(@ProjectMgmtID AS NVARCHAR(50)) + '/MS' + CAST(@MileStoneId AS NVARCHAR(50)) + '/TS' + CAST(@TaskId AS NVARCHAR(50)) + '/' + CAST(@IssueCount + 1 AS NVARCHAR(50));

        INSERT INTO IT.ProjectIssue (
            IssueCode,TaskId, ProjectMgmtID, SubTaskId, MileStoneId, ProjectLevel, 
            Description, Priority, Impact, DateOpened, DateClosed, 
            IssueOwner, Department, Status, Notes, AssignedTo, AssignedBy, 
            AssignedOn, CreatedBy, CreatedDt, ModifiedBy, ModifiedDt
        )
        VALUES (
            @IssueCode,@TaskId, @ProjectMgmtID, @SubTaskId, @MileStoneId, @ProjectLevel,
            @Description, @Priority, @Impact, @DateOpened, @DateClosed,
            @IssueOwner, @Department, @Status, @Notes, @AssignedTo, @AssignedBy,
            ISNULL(@AssignedOn, GETDATE()), @CreatedBy, ISNULL(@CreatedDt, GETDATE()), 
            @ModifiedBy, GETDATE()
        );
    END

    -- Update Operation (U)
    IF @Flag = 'U'
    BEGIN
        -- Ensure that the issueId exists
        IF @issueId IS NOT NULL
        BEGIN
            UPDATE IT.ProjectIssue
            SET 
                TaskId = COALESCE(NULLIF(@TaskId, NULL), TaskId),
                ProjectMgmtID = COALESCE(NULLIF(@ProjectMgmtID, NULL), ProjectMgmtID),
                SubTaskId = COALESCE(NULLIF(@SubTaskId, NULL), SubTaskId),
                MileStoneId = COALESCE(NULLIF(@MileStoneId, NULL), MileStoneId),
                ProjectLevel = COALESCE(NULLIF(@ProjectLevel, ''), ProjectLevel),
                Description = COALESCE(NULLIF(@Description, ''), Description),
                Priority = COALESCE(NULLIF(@Priority, ''), Priority),
                Impact = COALESCE(NULLIF(@Impact, ''), Impact),
                DateOpened = COALESCE(@DateOpened, DateOpened),
                DateClosed = COALESCE(@DateClosed, DateClosed),
                IssueOwner = COALESCE(NULLIF(@IssueOwner, NULL), IssueOwner),
                Department = COALESCE(NULLIF(@Department, ''), Department),
                Status = COALESCE(NULLIF(@Status, ''), Status),
                Notes = COALESCE(NULLIF(@Notes, ''), Notes),
                AssignedTo = COALESCE(NULLIF(@AssignedTo, NULL), AssignedTo),
                AssignedBy = COALESCE(NULLIF(@AssignedBy, NULL), AssignedBy),
                AssignedOn = COALESCE(@AssignedOn, AssignedOn),
                CreatedBy = COALESCE(NULLIF(@CreatedBy, NULL), CreatedBy),
                CreatedDt = COALESCE(@CreatedDt, CreatedDt),
                ModifiedBy = COALESCE(NULLIF(@ModifiedBy, NULL), ModifiedBy),
                ModifiedDt = GETDATE()
            WHERE issueId = @issueId;
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('issueId is required for update operation', 16, 1);
        END
    END

    -- Delete Operation (D)
    IF @Flag = 'D'
    BEGIN
        -- Ensure that the issueId exists
        IF @issueId IS NOT NULL
        BEGIN
            DELETE FROM IT.ProjectIssue
            WHERE issueId = @issueId;
        END
        ELSE
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('issueId is required for delete operation', 16, 1);
        END
    END
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_ManageProjectMembers]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO



CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_ManageProjectMembers]
    @Flag NVARCHAR(10),
    @PrMemberId INT = NULL,
    @ProjectMgmtID INT = NULL,
    @EmpID INT = NULL,
    @Role NVARCHAR(500) = NULL,
	@isResponsible [bit] NULL,
	@isAccountable [bit] NULL,
	@isConsulted [bit] NULL,
	@isInformed [bit] NULL,
    @Type NVARCHAR(500) = NULL,
    @CreatedBy INT = NULL,
    @CreatedDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @ModifiedBy INT = NULL,
    @ModifiedDt DATETIME = NULL,
	@errorMsg varchar(500) output
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Declare @count int
	
	select @count=count(EmpID) from [IT].[ProjectMembers] where EmpID=@EmpID and ProjectMgmtID=@ProjectMgmtID
	If @count>0 and @Flag = 'I'
	BEGIN
		
		Select @Flag = 'U' 
    END
	IF @Flag = 'I'

    BEGIN
			INSERT INTO [IT].[ProjectMembers]
			   ([ProjectMgmtID]
			   ,[EmpID]
			   ,[Role]
				,[Responsible]
				,[Accountable]
				,[Consulted]
				,[Informed]
				,[Type]
				,[CreatedBy]
				,[CreatedDt]
				,[ModifiedBy] 
				,[ModifiedDt]
				)
			VALUES
			   (
			   @ProjectMgmtID, 
			   @EmpID, 
			   @Role,
			   @isResponsible,
			   @isAccountable,
			   @isConsulted,
			   @isInformed, 
			   @Type, 
			   @CreatedBy, 
			   GETDATE(), 
			   NULL, 
			   GETDATE()
			   )
		
	END
    IF @Flag = 'U'
    BEGIN
        UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMembers]
        SET
            [ProjectMgmtID] = @ProjectMgmtID,
            [EmpID] =@EmpID,
            [Role] =@Role,
            [Type] =@Type,
			[Responsible] = @isResponsible,
			[Accountable] = @isAccountable,
			[Consulted] = @isConsulted,
			[Informed] = @isInformed,
            [ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
            [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
        WHERE [EmpID] = @EmpID and ProjectMgmtID=@ProjectMgmtID;
    END
	
	If @Flag='D'
	Begin
	if (@ProjectMgmtID is NULL or @ProjectMgmtID='') 
	select @ProjectMgmtID = ProjectMgmtID from IT.ProjectMembers where PrMemberId=@PrMemberId

		if @EmpID is NULL or @EmpID=''
		Begin
			select @EmpID =EmpID from IT.ProjectMembers where PrMemberId=@PrMemberId
		End
		
		select @count = count(ProjectOwner) from IT.ProjectMgmt
			where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID and CreatedBy=@EmpID
			If @count>0 
		Begin
			select @errorMsg='User has cant be deleted as he/she is creator of project'
			return 
		End
			
		select @count = count(ProjectOwner) from IT.ProjectMgmt
			where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID and @EmpID in (ProjectOwner, Sponser)		
		
		If @count>0 
		Begin
			select @errorMsg='User is either associated as Project Sponsor or Project Owner'
			return 
		End

		select @count= count(1) from IT.ProjectMilestone where owner=@EmpID and ProjectID = @ProjectMgmtID
		If @count>0 
		Begin
			select @errorMsg='User is associated to Milestone'
			return 
		End

		select @count= count(1) from IT.ProjectTask where assignTo=@EmpID  and  ProjectID =@ProjectMgmtID
		If @count>0 
		Begin
			select @errorMsg='User is associated to Task'
			return 
		End

		select @count=count(ProjectMgmtID) from IT.ProjectIssue where @EmpID in (AssignedBy, AssignedTo, IssueOwner) and  ProjectMgmtID=@ProjectMgmtID
		If @count>0 
		Begin
			select @errorMsg='User is associated to issue'
			return 
		End

		select @count = count(1) from IT.ProjectIssue
			where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID and (AssignedTo = @EmpID or AssignedBy = @EmpID or IssueOwner=@EmpID)		
		If @count>0 
		Begin
			select @errorMsg='User is associated to Issue'
			return 
		End
		
		Delete from IT.ProjectMembers where EmpID=@EmpID and ProjectMgmtID=@ProjectMgmtID

	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_ManageProjectTask]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_ManageProjectTask]
    @Flag CHAR(1),
    @TaskID INT = NULL,
    @MilestoneID INT,
    @ProjectID INT,
    @Owner INT,
    @EmpID INT,
    @AssignTo INT,
    @Duration INT,
    @Responsible BIT = NULL,
    @Accountable BIT = NULL,
    @Consulted BIT = NULL,
    @Informed BIT = NULL,
    @TaskTitle NVARCHAR(500) = NULL,
    @ProjectPhase NVARCHAR(500) = NULL,
    @TaskDesc NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @Priority NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @WorkHours NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @Status NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @CompletionDate DATETIME = NULL,
    @StartDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @EndDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @IsActive BIT = NULL,
    @IsSubtask BIT = NULL,
    @CreatedBy INT = NULL,
    @CreatedDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @ModifiedBy INT = NULL,
    @ModifiedDt DATETIME = NULL
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    IF @Flag = 'I'
    BEGIN
        INSERT INTO [IT].[ProjectTask]
        (
            [MilestoneID], 
            [ProjectID], 
            [Owner], 
            [EmpID], 
            [AssignTo], 
            [Duration], 
            [Responsible], 
            [Accountable], 
            [Consulted], 
            [Informed], 
            [TaskTitle], 
            [TaskDesc], 
            [Priority], 
            [WorkHours], 
            [Status], 
            [CompletionDate], 
            [StartDt], 
            [EndDt],
			[Projectphase],
            [IsActive], 
			[IsSubtask],
            [CreatedBy], 
            [CreatedDt]
        )
        VALUES
        (
            @MilestoneID, 
            @ProjectID, 
            @Owner, 
            @EmpID, 
            @AssignTo, 
            @Duration, 
            @Responsible, 
            @Accountable, 
            @Consulted, 
            @Informed, 
            @TaskTitle, 
            @TaskDesc, 
            @Priority, 
            @WorkHours, 
            @Status, 
            @CompletionDate, 
            @StartDt, 
            @EndDt, 
			@ProjectPhase,
            @IsActive, 
			@IsSubtask,
            @CreatedBy, 
            @CreatedDt
        );
    END
    ELSE IF @Flag = 'U'
    BEGIN
        IF @TaskID IS NULL
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('TaskID must be provided for update', 16, 1);
            RETURN;
        END

        UPDATE [IT].[ProjectTask]
        SET 
            [MilestoneID] = @MilestoneID,
            [ProjectID] = @ProjectID,
            [Owner] = @Owner,
            [EmpID] = @EmpID,
            [AssignTo] = @AssignTo,
            [Duration] = @Duration,
            [Responsible] = @Responsible,
            [Accountable] = @Accountable,
            [Consulted] = @Consulted,
            [Informed] = @Informed,
            [TaskTitle] = @TaskTitle,
            [TaskDesc] = @TaskDesc,
            [Priority] = @Priority,
            [WorkHours] = @WorkHours,
            [Status] = @Status,
            [CompletionDate] = @CompletionDate,
            [StartDt] = @StartDt,
            [EndDt] = @EndDt,
            [IsActive] = @IsActive,
            [ModifiedBy] = @ModifiedBy,
            [ModifiedDt] = @ModifiedDt,
			[IsSubtask] = @IsSubtask
        WHERE [TaskID] = @TaskID;
    END
    ELSE IF @Flag = 'D'  -- Delete operation
    BEGIN
        IF @TaskID IS NULL
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('TaskID must be provided for delete', 16, 1);
            RETURN;
        END

        DELETE FROM [IT].[ProjectTask]
        WHERE [TaskID] = @TaskID;
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        RAISERROR('Invalid flag provided. Use I for Insert, U for Update, or D for Delete.', 16, 1);
    END
END;
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
create PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_Module](
	@Flag [char](1),
	@SupportID [int] NULL,
	@SupportName nchar(500) NULL,
	@ParentID [int] NULL,
	@IsActive bit NULL,
	@CreatedBy int NULL,
	@CreatedDate datetime NULL,
	@UpdatedBy int NULL,
	@UpdatedDate datetime NULL
	
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert CR Release Fields
	BEGIN 
		BEGIN TRANSACTION

		
			INSERT INTO [IT].[Support] (
			[SupportName],
			[ParentID],
			[IsActive],
			[CreatedBy],
			[CreatedDate]
		 )
			VALUES (
			@SupportName,
			@ParentID,
			@IsActive,
			@CreatedBy,
			getdate()
			)
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[Support] SET
				[SupportName]=@SupportName,
				[ParentID]=@ParentID,
				[IsActive]=@IsActive,
				[UpdatedBy]=@UpdatedBy,
				[UpdatedDate]=getdate()
			WHERE SupportID=@SupportID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete CR Approver Field
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			DELETE FROM [IT].[Support] WHERE SupportID=@SupportID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('Refrence Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,Yavanthi Shivakumar>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_NatureofChange](
	@Flag [char](1),
	@NatureofChangeID [int] NULL,
	@CategoryID [int] NULL,
	@NatureofChange[nvarchar](MAX) NULL,
	@IsActive [bit] NULL,
	@CreatedBy [int] NULL,
	@CreatedDate [datetime] NULL,
	@ModifiedBy [int] NULL,
	@ModifiedDate [datetime] NULL
	
	)
AS
BEGIN 
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert CR Release Fields
	BEGIN 
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
		
		
			INSERT INTO [IT].[NatureofChange] (
			[CategoryID],
			[NatureofChange],
			[IsActive],
			[CreatedBy],
			[CreatedDate]
		 )
			VALUES (
			@CategoryID,
			@NatureofChange,
			@IsActive,
			@CreatedBy,
			getdate()
			)
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			UPDATE [IT].[NatureofChange] SET
				[CategoryID]=@CategoryID,
				[NatureofChange]=@NatureofChange,
				[IsActive]=@IsActive,
				[ModifiedBy]=@ModifiedBy,
				[ModifiedDate]=getdate()
			WHERE NatureofChangeID=@NatureofChangeID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag = 'D' -- Delete CR Approver Field
BEGIN
    BEGIN TRANSACTION
    -- Check if NatureofChangeID is linked in another table
    IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM ChangeRequest WHERE NatureOfChange = @NatureofChangeID)
    BEGIN
        -- NatureofChangeID is linked, raise an error message
        ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
        RAISERROR('The NatureofChangeID is mapped in another table and cannot be deleted.', 16, 1)
        RETURN
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        -- NatureofChangeID is not linked, proceed with deletion
        DELETE FROM [IT].[NatureofChange] WHERE NatureofChangeID = @NatureofChangeID
        COMMIT TRANSACTION
    END
END
ELSE
    RETURN ERROR_MESSAGE()
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		
			raiserror ('NatureofChange Transaction Error :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_PMilestone]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_PMilestone]
    @Flag CHAR(1), -- I for Insert, U for Update, D for Delete
    @ProjMilestoneID INT = NULL, -- For Update and Delete
    @ProjectID INT,
    @MilestoneTitle NVARCHAR(500) = NULL,
    @MilestoneDesc NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @MilestoneStatus NVARCHAR(500) = NULL,
    @Owner int = NULL,
    @Priority NVARCHAR(500) = NULL,
    @StartDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @EndDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @ActualStartDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @ActualEndDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @FinishStartDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @FinishEndDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @ActualFinishStartDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @ActualFinishEndDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @IsActive BIT = NULL,
    @CreatedBy INT = NULL,
    @ModifiedBy INT = NULL,
	@Error varchar(50) output
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Declare @count int, @taskcount int
	
	
    IF @Flag = 'I' -- Insert Operation
    BEGIN
		Select @count= count(1) from it.ProjectMilestone where [ProjectID]=@ProjectID and MilestoneTitle=@MilestoneTitle
		if @count>0
		Begin
			select @Error='Milestone Title exists'
			Return
		End

        INSERT INTO [IT].[ProjectMilestone] 
        (
            [ProjectID],
            [MilestoneTitle],
            [MilestoneDesc],
            [MilestoneStatus],
            [Owner],
            [Priority],
            [StartDt],
            [EndDt],
            [ActualStartDt],
            [ActualEndDt],
            [FinishStartDt],
            [FinishEndDt],
            [ActualFinishStartDt],
            [ActualFinishEndDt],
            [IsActive],
            [CreatedBy],
            [CreatedDt],
            [ModifiedBy],
            [ModifiedDt]
        )
        VALUES 
        (
            @ProjectID,
            @MilestoneTitle,
            @MilestoneDesc,
            @MilestoneStatus,
            @Owner,
            @Priority,
            @StartDt,
            @EndDt,
            @ActualStartDt,
            @ActualEndDt,
            @FinishStartDt,
            @FinishEndDt,
            @ActualFinishStartDt,
            @ActualFinishEndDt,
            @IsActive,
            @CreatedBy,
            GETDATE(), -- Automatically set Created Date
            @ModifiedBy,
            NULL -- Modified Date is NULL for Insert
        );
		UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
		SET
		[Activity] = 'Project Milestone Created',
		[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
        [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
		where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectID
    END

    IF @Flag = 'U' -- Update Operation
    BEGIN

		Select @count= count(ProjectID) from it.ProjectTask where [ProjectID]=@ProjectID and MilestoneID=@ProjMilestoneID
		if @count>0
		Begin
			
			select @taskcount=count(TaskID) from it.ProjectTask where [ProjectID]=@ProjectID and MilestoneID=@ProjMilestoneID and status='Resolved'
			if @count!=@taskcount and  @MilestoneStatus='Completed'
			Begin
				select @Error='Task should be resolved before closure!'
				Return
			End
		End

        UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMilestone]
        SET
            [ProjectID] = @ProjectID,
            [MilestoneTitle] = @MilestoneTitle,
            [MilestoneDesc] = @MilestoneDesc,
            [MilestoneStatus] = @MilestoneStatus,
            [Owner] = @Owner,
            [Priority] = @Priority,
            [StartDt] = @StartDt,
            [EndDt] = @EndDt,
            [ActualStartDt] = @ActualStartDt,
            [ActualEndDt] = @ActualEndDt,
            [FinishStartDt] = @FinishStartDt,
            [FinishEndDt] = @FinishEndDt,
            [ActualFinishStartDt] = @ActualFinishStartDt,
            [ActualFinishEndDt] = @ActualFinishEndDt,
            [IsActive] = @IsActive,
            [CreatedDt] = (SELECT CreatedDt FROM [IT].[ProjectMilestone] WHERE ProjMilestoneID = @ProjMilestoneID), -- Keep original Created Date
            [ModifiedBy] = @ModifiedBy,
            [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
        WHERE [ProjMilestoneID] = @ProjMilestoneID;
    END

    IF @Flag = 'D'
    BEGIN
	
			select @taskcount=count(TaskID) from it.ProjectTask where [ProjectID]=@ProjectID and MilestoneID=@ProjMilestoneID
			if @taskcount>0
			Begin
				select @Error='Cannot delete milestone as task is associated to it!'
				Return
			End
        DELETE FROM [IT].[ProjectMilestone]
        WHERE [ProjMilestoneID] = @ProjMilestoneID;
    END
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_pmMaster]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_pmMaster]
    @Flag CHAR(1),
    @ProjectID INT = NULL,
    @ProjectName VARCHAR(500) = NULL,
    @ProjectDesc VARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @ProjectGroup VARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @ProjectAccess VARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @Deliverables VARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @ProjectOwner INT = NULL,
    @StartDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @EndDt DATETIME = NULL,
    @isStrict BIT = NULL,
    @IsActive BIT = NULL,
    @CreatedBy INT = NULL,
    @ModifiedBy INT = NULL
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert operation
    IF @Flag = 'I'
    BEGIN
        INSERT INTO [IT].[pmMaster] (
            [ProjectName],
            [ProjectDesc],
            [ProjectGroup],
            [ProjectAccess],
            [Deliverables],
            [ProjectOwner],
            [StartDt],
            [EndDt],
            [isStrict],
            [IsActive],
            [CreatedBy],
            [CreatedDt],
            [ModifiedBy],
            [ModifiedDt]
        )
        VALUES (
            @ProjectName,
            @ProjectDesc,
            @ProjectGroup,
            @ProjectAccess,
            @Deliverables,
            @ProjectOwner,
            @StartDt,
            @EndDt,
            @isStrict,
            @IsActive,
            @CreatedBy,
            GETDATE(),
            @ModifiedBy,
            GETDATE()
        );
    END

    -- Update operation
    ELSE IF @Flag = 'U'
    BEGIN
        IF @ProjectID IS NULL
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('ProjectID is required for Update operation.', 16, 1);
            RETURN;
        END

        UPDATE [IT].[pmMaster]
        SET
            [ProjectName] = CASE WHEN @ProjectName IS NOT NULL THEN @ProjectName ELSE [ProjectName] END,
            [ProjectDesc] = CASE WHEN @ProjectDesc IS NOT NULL THEN @ProjectDesc ELSE [ProjectDesc] END,
            [ProjectGroup] = CASE WHEN @ProjectGroup IS NOT NULL THEN @ProjectGroup ELSE [ProjectGroup] END,
            [ProjectAccess] = CASE WHEN @ProjectAccess IS NOT NULL THEN @ProjectAccess ELSE [ProjectAccess] END,
            [Deliverables] = CASE WHEN @Deliverables IS NOT NULL THEN @Deliverables ELSE [Deliverables] END,
            [ProjectOwner] = CASE WHEN @ProjectOwner IS NOT NULL THEN @ProjectOwner ELSE [ProjectOwner] END,
            [StartDt] = CASE WHEN @StartDt IS NOT NULL THEN @StartDt ELSE [StartDt] END,
            [EndDt] = CASE WHEN @EndDt IS NOT NULL THEN @EndDt ELSE [EndDt] END,
            [isStrict] = CASE WHEN @isStrict IS NOT NULL THEN @isStrict ELSE [isStrict] END,
            [IsActive] = CASE WHEN @IsActive IS NOT NULL THEN @IsActive ELSE [IsActive] END,
            [ModifiedBy] = @ModifiedBy,
            [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
        WHERE [ProjectID] = @ProjectID;
    END

    ELSE IF @Flag = 'D'
    BEGIN
        IF @ProjectID IS NULL
        BEGIN
            RAISERROR('ProjectID is required for Delete operation.', 16, 1);
            RETURN;
        END

        DELETE FROM [IT].[pmMaster]
        WHERE [ProjectID] = @ProjectID;
    END

    ELSE
    BEGIN
        RAISERROR('Invalid flag. Use "I" for Insert, "U" for Update, or "D" for Delete.', 16, 1);
        RETURN;
    END
END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_PRApprover]
	@ProjectMgmtID int,
	@ApprLevel int ,
	@Approver1Remark nvarchar(Max),
	@Approver2Remark nvarchar(max),
	@Status nvarchar(100),
	@Approver2 int,
	@Approver1 int
AS
BEGIN

	Declare @Activity Varchar(100)

	if @Status='In Progress' 
		select @Activity='Project Closure Rejected'
	else 
		select @Activity='Project Closure Approved'
	IF @ApprLevel = 1
	BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
		UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
		SET
		Approver1Remark =@Approver1Remark,
		Status = @Status,
		Activity = @Activity,
		Approver1 = @Approver1,
		ModifiedBy = @Approver1,
		ModifiedDt = GetDate()
		WHERE ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID
	END


	
	IF @ApprLevel = 2
	BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
	SET
	Approver2Remark = @Approver2Remark,
	Status = @Status,
	Activity = @Activity,
	Approver2 = @Approver2,
	ModifiedBy = @Approver2,
	ModifiedDt = GetDate()

	WHERE ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID
	END
END
GO

	)

		 )

				[UpdatedBy]=@UpdatedBy,

	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)

SET ANSI_NULLS ON

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_PRLesson]
	@Flag char(1),
	@PRLessonsID [int],
	@ProjectID [int] NULL,
	@TemplateID [int] NULL,
	@TaskID [int] NULL,
	@MilestoneID [int] NULL,
	@Category [nvarchar](250) NULL,
	@Lessons_Type [nvarchar](max) NULL,
	@Description [nvarchar](max) NULL,
	@ProjCloserAccept [varchar](50) NULL,
	@Impact [nvarchar](max) NULL,
	@Recommendation [nvarchar](max) NULL,
	@CreatedBy [int]
AS
BEGIN
	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN
			SET NOCOUNT ON;
			IF @Flag = 'I'
				BEGIN	

					INSERT INTO [IT].[PRLesson](
					   [ProjectID]
					  ,[TemplateID]
					  ,[TaskID]
					  ,[MilestoneID]
					  ,[Category]
					  ,[Lessons_Type]
					  ,[Description]
					  ,[Impact]
					  ,[Recommendation]
					  ,[ProjCloserAccept]
					  ,[CreatedBy]
					  ,[CreatedDt]
					)
					VALUES(
					    @ProjectID
					   ,@TemplateID
					   ,@TaskID
					   ,@MilestoneID
					   ,@Category
					   ,@Lessons_Type
					   ,@Description
					   ,@Impact
					   ,@Recommendation
					   ,@ProjCloserAccept
					   ,@CreatedBy
					   ,GETDATE()
					)
					Declare @llID int
					select @llID = max(PRLessonsID) from IT.PRLesson where ProjectID=@ProjectID and TemplateID=@TemplateID 
					
					update [IT].[PRTemplateResponse] set LessonLearnedID=@llID where PrId=@ProjectID and TemplateID=@TemplateID

			
					
					UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
					SET
					[Activity] = 'Project Lesson Created',
					[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
					[ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
					where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectID
				END
			ELSE IF @Flag = 'U'
				BEGIN
					UPDATE [IT].[PRLesson] SET
					   [ProjectID]		 = @ProjectID
					  ,[TemplateID]      = @TemplateID
					  ,[TaskID]			 = @TaskID
					  ,[MilestoneID]	 = @MilestoneID
					  ,[Category]		 = @Category
					  ,[Lessons_Type]	 = @Lessons_Type
					  ,[Description]	 = @Description
					  ,[Impact]			 = @Impact
					  ,[Recommendation]	 = @Recommendation
					  ,[ProjCloserAccept] =@ProjCloserAccept
					  ,[ModifiedBy]		 = @CreatedBy
					  ,[ModifiedDt]		 = GETDATE()
					  WHERE PRLessonsID	 = @PRLessonsID
				UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
					SET
					[Activity] = 'Project Lesson Updated',
					[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
					[ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
					where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectID
				END
			ELSE IF @Flag = 'D'
				BEGIN
					DELETE FROM [IT].[PRLesson] WHERE PRLessonsID = @PRLessonsID
					UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
					SET
					[Activity] = 'Project Lesson Deleted',
					[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
					[ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
					where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectID
				END
		END
	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_ProjectClosure]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_ProjectClosure]
	@Flag char(1),
	@ClosureID [int],
	@ProjectID [int],
	@Status  [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Remarks [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Attachment  [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@LessonsLearnt  [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Task  [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Category  [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@ProblemsStatement  [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Impact  [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Recommendation  [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@Feedback  [nvarchar](500) NULL,
	@IsSponsor [BIT] NULL,
	@CreatedBy [int]	
	--@errMsg [nvarchar](500) NULL OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
BEGIN TRY
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Declare @mcount int, @tcount int, @errMsg varchar(50), @Activity varchar(100),@count int

	select @count=count(ProjectID) from IT.ProjectClosure where ProjectID=@ProjectID
	If (@count>0)  
	Begin
		set @Flag = 'U'
		Select @ClosureID=ClosureID from IT.ProjectClosure where ProjectID=@ProjectID
	End

	BEGIN TRANSACTION
	select @mcount=count(*) from IT.ProjectMilestone where ProjectID=@ProjectID and (status!='Completed' or status!='Cancelled')
	select @tcount=count(*) from IT.ProjectTask where ProjectID=@ProjectID and status!='Resolved'
	if (@tcount>0 or @mcount>0) and @Status='Completed'
	Begin
		select @errMsg='Alert'
		raiserror (@errMsg,16,1,'Project Closure');
		return
	End
	
	if @status='In Progress'
		select @Activity='Project Closure Rejected'
	else
		select @Activity='Project Closure Created'

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
	IF @Flag = 'I'	
	BEGIN 
		
			INSERT INTO [IT].[ProjectClosure](
			   [ProjectID]
			  ,[Status]
			  ,[Remarks]
			  ,[Attachment]
			  ,[LessonsLearnt]
			  ,[Task]
			  ,[Category]
			  ,[ProblemsStatement]
			  ,[Impact]
			  ,[Recommendation]
			  ,[Feedback]
			  ,[IsSponsor]
			  ,[CreatedBy]
			  ,[CreatedDt]
			)
			VALUES(
			  @ProjectID,
			  @Status,
			  @Remarks,
			  @Attachment,
			  @LessonsLearnt,
			  @Task,
			  @Category,
			  @ProblemsStatement,
			  @Impact,
			  @Recommendation,
			  @Feedback,
			  @IsSponsor,
			  @CreatedBy,
			  GETDATE()
			  )
		UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
		SET
		[Activity] = @Activity,
		[Status] = @Status,
		[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
        [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
		where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='U' -- Update CR Approver Fieldss
	BEGIN
		
			UPDATE [IT].[ProjectClosure] SET
				[Status]            =@Status
			  ,[Remarks]			=@Remarks
			  ,[Attachment]			=@Attachment
			  ,[LessonsLearnt]		=@LessonsLearnt
			  ,[Task]				=@Task
			  ,[Category]			=@Category
			  ,[ProblemsStatement]	=@ProblemsStatement
			  ,[Impact]				=@Impact
			  ,[Recommendation]		=@Recommendation
			  ,[Feedback]			=@Feedback
			  ,[IsSponsor]			=@IsSponsor
			  ,[ModifiedBy]			=@CreatedBy
			  ,[ModifiedDt]			=GETDATE()
			  Where ClosureID =@ClosureID;

			 UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
			SET
			[Activity] = @Activity,
			[Status] = @Status,
		    [ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
            [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
		    where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectID
			  COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE IF @Flag='D'   -- Delete CR Approver Field
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRANSACTION
			DELETE FROM [IT].[ProjectClosure] WHERE  ClosureID =@ClosureID;
			UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
		SET
		[Activity] = 'Project Issue Deleted',
		[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
        [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
		where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectID
		COMMIT TRANSACTION
	END
	ELSE
		RETURN error_message()
END TRY
	
BEGIN CATCH
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @err_num int, @err_msg varchar(100)
			select @err_num=ERROR_NUMBER()
			select @err_msg=ERROR_MESSAGE()
		    if @errMsg=''
				raiserror ('Project Closure Error! :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
			else
				raiserror ('Project Task or Milestone should be Completed or Cancelled before closure! :%d: %s',16,1,@err_num,@err_msg);
		END
END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[SP_ProjectGroup]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[SP_ProjectGroup]
    @Flag CHAR(1),
	@ProjectGroupID INT = NULL,
	@ProjectGroupName VARCHAR(1000) = NULL,
	@IsActive BIT = NULL,
    @CreatedBy INT = NULL,
    @ModifiedBy INT = NULL,
	@Error Varchar(50) Output
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
	DECLARE @count int;
    IF @Flag = 'I'
		BEGIN
			Select @count= count(1) from it.[ProjectGroup] where [ProjectGroupName]=@ProjectGroupName
			if @count>0
			Begin
				select @Error='Duplicate Project Group Name!'
				Return
			End
			INSERT INTO [IT].[ProjectGroup] ([ProjectGroupName], [IsActive], [CreatedBy], [CreatedDt])
			VALUES (@ProjectGroupName, @IsActive, @CreatedBy, GETDATE());
        
			SELECT SCOPE_IDENTITY() AS NewProjectGroupID;  -- Return the newly inserted ID
		END

    ELSE IF @Flag = 'U'
    BEGIN
        UPDATE [IT].[ProjectGroup]
        SET 
            [ProjectGroupName] = @ProjectGroupName,
            [IsActive] = @IsActive,
            [ModifiedBy] = @ModifiedBy,
            [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
        WHERE [ProjectGroupID] = @ProjectGroupID;
    END

    ELSE IF @Flag = 'D'
    BEGIN
        DELETE FROM [IT].[ProjectGroup]
        WHERE [ProjectGroupID] = @ProjectGroupID;
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        PRINT 'Invalid Operation Type';
    END
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [IT].[sp_ProjectIssue]    Script Date: 26-02-2026 21:13:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [IT].[sp_ProjectIssue]
    @Flag CHAR(1),
    @IssueID INT = NULL, 
    @ProjectMgmtID INT = NULL,
    @TaskID INT = NULL,
    @SubTaskID INT = NULL,
    @MilestoneID INT = NULL,
    @ProjectLevel NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @Description NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @Priority NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @Impact NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @DateOpened DATETIME = NULL,
	@CompletionDate DATETIME = NULL,
    @DateClosed DATETIME = NULL,
    @IssueOwner INT = NULL,
    @Department NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @Status NVARCHAR(200) = NULL,
    @Notes NVARCHAR(2000) = NULL,
    @AssignedTo INT = NULL,
    @AssignedBy INT = NULL,
    @AssignedOn DATETIME = NULL,
    @CreatedBy INT = NULL
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Declare
	@IssueCode varchar(20),
	@MaxCount varchar(4),
	@return_value varchar(20),
	@err_num int,
	@err_msg varchar(100)
    -- Insert Operation
    IF @Flag = 'I'
    BEGIN
		select @MaxCount = count(issueId)+1 from [IT].[ProjectIssue]
		select @IssueCode= CONCAT ('PR',@ProjectMgmtID,'/','MS',@MilestoneID,'/','TS',@TaskID,'/',@MaxCount)
        INSERT INTO [IT].[ProjectIssue]
        (
			[IssueCode],
            [ProjectMgmtID],
            [TaskID],
            [SubTaskID],
            [MileStoneID],
            [ProjectLevel],
            [Description],
            [Priority],
            [Impact],
            [DateOpened],
			[CompletionDate],
            [DateClosed],
            [IssueOwner],
            [Department],
            [Status],
            [Notes],
            [AssignedTo],
            [AssignedBy],
            [AssignedOn],
            [CreatedBy],
            [CreatedDt]
        )
        VALUES
        (
			@IssueCode,
            @ProjectMgmtID,
            @TaskID,
            @SubTaskID,
            @MilestoneID,
            @ProjectLevel,
            @Description,
            @Priority,
            @Impact,
            @DateOpened,
			@CompletionDate,
            @DateClosed,
            @IssueOwner,
            @Department,
            @Status,
            @Notes,
            @AssignedTo,
            @AssignedBy,
            @AssignedOn,
            @CreatedBy,
            GetDate()
        )
		UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
		SET
		[Activity] = 'Project Issue Created',
		[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
        [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
		where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID
    END

    IF @Flag = 'U'
    BEGIN
        UPDATE [IT].[ProjectIssue]
        SET
            [ProjectMgmtID] = CASE WHEN @ProjectMgmtID IS NOT NULL THEN @ProjectMgmtID ELSE [ProjectMgmtID] END,
            [TaskID] = CASE WHEN @TaskID IS NOT NULL THEN @TaskID ELSE [TaskID] END,
            [SubTaskID] = CASE WHEN @SubTaskID IS NOT NULL THEN @SubTaskID ELSE [SubTaskID] END,
            [MileStoneID] = CASE WHEN @MilestoneID IS NOT NULL THEN @MilestoneID ELSE [MileStoneID] END,
            [ProjectLevel] = CASE WHEN @ProjectLevel IS NOT NULL THEN @ProjectLevel ELSE [ProjectLevel] END,
            [Description] = CASE WHEN @Description IS NOT NULL THEN @Description ELSE [Description] END,
            [Priority] = CASE WHEN @Priority IS NOT NULL THEN @Priority ELSE [Priority] END,
            [Impact] = CASE WHEN @Impact IS NOT NULL THEN @Impact ELSE [Impact] END,
            [DateOpened] = CASE WHEN @DateOpened IS NOT NULL THEN @DateOpened ELSE [DateOpened] END,
			[CompletionDate] = CASE WHEN @CompletionDate IS NOT NULL THEN @CompletionDate ELSE [CompletionDate] END,
            [DateClosed] = CASE WHEN @DateClosed IS NOT NULL THEN @DateClosed ELSE [DateClosed] END,
            [IssueOwner] = CASE WHEN @IssueOwner IS NOT NULL THEN @IssueOwner ELSE [IssueOwner] END,
            [Department] = CASE WHEN @Department IS NOT NULL THEN @Department ELSE [Department] END,
            [Status] = CASE WHEN @Status IS NOT NULL THEN @Status ELSE [Status] END,
            [Notes] = CASE WHEN @Notes IS NOT NULL THEN @Notes ELSE [Notes] END,
            [AssignedTo] = CASE WHEN @AssignedTo IS NOT NULL THEN @AssignedTo ELSE [AssignedTo] END,
            [AssignedBy] = CASE WHEN @AssignedBy IS NOT NULL THEN @AssignedBy ELSE [AssignedBy] END,
            [AssignedOn] = CASE WHEN @AssignedOn IS NOT NULL THEN @AssignedOn ELSE [AssignedOn] END,
            [ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
            [ModifiedDt] = GetDate()
        WHERE [issueId] = @IssueID
		UPDATE [IT].[ProjectMgmt]
		SET
		[Activity] = 'Project Issue Updated',
		[ModifiedBy] = @CreatedBy,
        [ModifiedDt] = GETDATE()
		where ProjectMgmtID = @ProjectMgmtID
    END

    IF @Flag = 'D'
    BEGIN
        DELETE FROM [IT].[ProjectIssue]
        WHERE [issueId] = @IssueID
    END

END
GO
